<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покраснеть.html>покрасне́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokrasnétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покраснение.html>покрасне́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokrasnénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покраснение.html>покрасне́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покраснение.html>покрасне́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покраснение.html>покрасне́ний</a></b>)

***покраснеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покраснеть.html>покрасне́ть</a> (3109)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:краснеть.html>красне́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krasnétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покраснеть.html>покрасне́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokrasnétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:краснеть.html>красне́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to redden, to grow red</li>
<li>to blush, to turn red in the face</li></ol>

***покрикивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покрикивать.html>покри́кивать</a> (11765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крикнуть.html>кри́кнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kríknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрикивать.html>покри́кивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokríkivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to hout <i>(at)</i>, to command around</li>
<li>to chide, to scold</li>
<li>to shriek, to yelp</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кричать.html>крича́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kričátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крикнуть.html>кри́кнуть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kríknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крик.html>крик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крикливый.html>крикли́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kriklívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покричать.html>покрича́ть</a> (20296)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кричать.html>крича́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kričátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покричать.html>покрича́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokričátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кричать.html>крича́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покров.html>покро́в</a> (6371)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыть.html>покры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokrýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кров.html>кров</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krov</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покров.html>покро́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokróv</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покров.html>покро́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покров.html>покро́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покров.html>покро́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cover, covering
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:покров.html>покро́вом</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>но́чи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pod <b>pokróvom</b> nóči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at night</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">under <b>cover</b> of night</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:покров.html>покро́вом</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pod <b>pokróvom</b> tájny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">secretly</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">under <b>cover</b> of secrecy</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волосяной.html>волосяно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:покров.html>покро́в</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">volosjanój <b>pokróv</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">hair <b>covering</b>, pelage</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>hearse cloth</li></ol>

***покровитель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покровитель.html>покрови́тель</a> (10373)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрывать.html>покрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokryvátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">er</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покровитель.html>покрови́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokrovítelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покровитель.html>покрови́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покровитель.html>покрови́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покровитель.html>покрови́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">покрови́тельница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>patron, protector, sponsor</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутить.html>крути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрутить.html>покрути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokrutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутить.html>крути́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to twist, to turn, to rotate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play around <i>(with smb)</i>, to have an affair <i>(with smb)</i></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыть.html>покры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokrýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрывать.html>покрыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokryvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыть.html>покры́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cover</li>
<li>to drown out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">agriculture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mount <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">an animal to mate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покрываться.html>покрыва́ться</a> (8999)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрывать.html>покрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрываться.html>покрыва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokryvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыться.html>покры́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cover oneself, to get covered</li>
<li>to be covered <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покрываться.html>покрыва́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:корка.html>ко́ркой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokryvátʹsja</b> kórkoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to crust; get crusted over</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покрываться.html>покрыва́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пена.html>пе́ной</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokryvátʹsja</b> pénoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scum; mantle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покрываться.html>покрыва́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>ли́стьями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokryvátʹsja</b> lístʹjami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be covered with leaves</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрывать.html>покрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыть.html>покры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokrýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрытие.html>покры́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokrýtije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрытие.html>покры́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрытие.html>покры́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрытие.html>покры́тий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>covering, coating
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покрытие.html>покры́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ши</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokrýtije</b> krýši</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">roofing</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покрытие.html>покры́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ги</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokrýtije</b> dorógi</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">road surfacing</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>coat, surface

<li>discharge, payment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покрытие.html>покры́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:расход.html>расхо́дов</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokrýtije</b> rasxódov</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">defrayment/defrayal of expenses</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

***покрыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покрыть.html>покры́ть</a> (1920)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыть.html>покры́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokrýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрывать.html>покрыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cover, to roof (<i>a house</i>) ; to thatch, to tile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыть.html>покры́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шифер.html>ши́фером</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokrýtʹ</b> šíferom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slate</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to coat (<i>with paint</i>)</li>
<li>to cover, to trump (<i>in card games</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нечего.html>не́чем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú néčem <b>krytʹ</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he hasn't a leg to stand on, there's nothing he can say to that (<i>original meaning: he has no (good) card to cover</i> (<i>colloquial</i>)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scold, to rail (at), to swear (at)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыть.html>покры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokrýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыться.html>покры́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokrýtʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыться.html>кры́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрываться.html>покрыва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cover oneself, to get covered</li>
<li>to be covered <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыться.html>покры́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:корка.html>ко́ркой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokrýtʹsja</b> kórkoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to crust; get crusted over</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыться.html>покры́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пена.html>пе́ной</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokrýtʹsja</b> pénoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scum; mantle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыться.html>покры́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>ли́стьями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokrýtʹsja</b> lístʹjami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be covered with leaves</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бо</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыться.html>покры́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туча.html>ту́чами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nébo <b>pokrýlosʹ</b> túčami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the sky became cloudy [clouded over]</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыться.html>покры́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:румянец.html>румя́нцем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokrýtʹsja</b> rumjáncem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to blush, glow, be flushed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыть.html>покры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokrýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***покупавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покупать.html>покупа́вший</a> (1939)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покупать.html>покупа́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokupávšij</span>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покупать.html>покупа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokupátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to buy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>to sell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́ры</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:покупаться.html>покупа́ются</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éti továry xorošó <b>pokupájutsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">these goods sell well</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покупать.html>покупа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokupátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to buy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
